<article id="post-108" class="post-108 page type-page status-publish hentry without-featured-image">
	<header class="entry-header">
		<h1 class="entry-title">Context &#8211; Fantasy</h1>	</header>
		<div class="entry-content">
			<p>Fantasy Mindmap:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="184" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/fantasy-mindmap/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png" data-orig-size="1204,675" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Fantasy Mindmap" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=825" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-184" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=825" alt="Fantasy Mindmap.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png 1204w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=150&amp;h=84 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=300&amp;h=168 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=768&amp;h=431 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=1024&amp;h=574 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1204px) 100vw, 1204px" /></p>
<p>Here are a bunch of words I associate with the word fantasy. I started with words like magic, medieval, heroes as these are words that immediately sprung to mind, following this I went with monsters, dungeons, and towns as these are some other quite common things found in fantasy. With a couple words down on the page I moved onto looking at words I could associate with these, like different types of monsters, things to do with magic, things you&#8217;d find in and around a town like a castle, with castle came kings, queens and knights. A lot of this I find to be very much related to fantasy but most of all would be magic, it is by far one of my favourite things to do with fantasy. Magic is a very vast subject with many different types and forms. Magic has sprung a whole load of different films, books, games, pictures, music, it&#8217;s very closely linked to all media as you have a wide option as to what you want to do.</p>
<p>Tomes Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="189" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/tomes-moodboard-4/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg" data-orig-size="1219,584" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Tomes Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=825" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-189" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=825" alt="Tomes Moodboard.jpg"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg 1219w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=150&amp;h=72 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=300&amp;h=144 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=768&amp;h=368 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=1024&amp;h=491 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1219px) 100vw, 1219px" /></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>The reason I like these images of tomes as a collective is that they all show different styles of designs on the covers as they could have just been a large book. This is the kind of thing I would like to include in my fantasy environment, which would probably be the common shade of green shown above as itâ€™s the most traditional along with the gold to create various detail and designs on the front.</p>
<p>Bows Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="190" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/bows-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1215,584" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Bows Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=825" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-190" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Bows Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png 1215w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=72 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=144 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=369 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=492 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1215px) 100vw, 1215px" /></p>
<p>These Â bows appealed to me as I like the level of appendages on each bow to give it a more grand and special look to it as opposed to a more standard bow which doesnâ€™t look all that interesting. As a collective I like the colours that are used for example the oranges, blues, golds, and yellows. A lot of the images here display bird like features which is another thing that really appealed to me and if I were to include a bow in my environment I would do this myself.</p>
<p>Gargoyles Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="191" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/gargoyles-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1219,568" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Gargoyles Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=825" loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-191" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Gargoyles Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png 1219w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=70 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=140 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=358 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=477 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1219px) 100vw, 1219px" /></p>
<p>Gargoyles have always been a fascinating aspect of gothic architecture due to its many different and unique forms. I like the visuals of these gargoyles as they all display a level of demonic aura which makes for a ominous grin of deceit. This is something that if I were to include a gargoyle into my work would be an aspect of which Iâ€™d aspire to achieve.</p>
<p>Rings Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="192" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/rings-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1222,612" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Rings Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=825" loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-192" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Rings Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png 1222w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=75 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=150 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=385 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=513 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1222px) 100vw, 1222px" /></p>
<p>Here are a selection of images showing rings. I like these rings because they have a very mystical look to them, with the intricate designs and the effective use of jewels they look like magical rings which have been a feature in games featuring magic for a long time, that being if they give a buff or if they cast a spell either one is used frequently. I quite like the idea of having a ring in my diorama if it were to be a magical study or a wizards cabin, or even just in a cave, on the ground as treasure to be found.</p>
<p>Crystals Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="193" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/crystals-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1207,683" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Crystals Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=825" loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-193" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Crystals Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png 1207w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=85 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=170 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=435 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=579 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1207px) 100vw, 1207px" /></p>
<p>I like the idea of having crystals in a fantasy environment, especially if it were to be a crystal cave like scene showing different bright magically crystals in a undisturbed place, a secret abode for fairies and pixies maybe. If I were to have crystals I&#8217;d make them a variety of different colours not just purple and blue, the reason I chose these images is that I like the shapes of them and could use them in my idea, I also like the density of each one maybe with smaller crystals being in larger swarms and larger crystals being on their own.</p>
<p>Caves Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="195" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/caves-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1215,666" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Caves Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=825" loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-195" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Caves Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png 1215w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=82 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=164 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=421 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=561 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1215px) 100vw, 1215px" />Here are some images of caves, the reason I chose these images is that I like the way they depicted a cave. I am quite inspired to create a diorama of a magic cave, as previously shown I would like it to be a crystal cave as it sounds really interesting to me. I would model it after the last two images which show the crystals lighting up the cave and creating a nice ambient light. The variety of shapes will be greatly increased when I do it as I&#8217;d like to have different types of crystal clusters. Despite saying I&#8217;d use different colours I do quite like the purple blue colour scheme as it contrasts nicely.</p>

		<!-- CCPA [start] -->
		<script type="text/javascript">
			( function () {

				var setupPrivacy = function() {

					// Minimal Mozilla Cookie library
					// https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Document/cookie/Simple_document.cookie_framework
					var cookieLib = window.cookieLib = {getItem:function(e){return e&&decodeURIComponent(document.cookie.replace(new RegExp("(?:(?:^|.*;)\\s*"+encodeURIComponent(e).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g,"\\$&")+"\\s*\\=\\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$"),"$1"))||null},setItem:function(e,o,n,t,r,i){if(!e||/^(?:expires|max\-age|path|domain|secure)$/i.test(e))return!1;var c="";if(n)switch(n.constructor){case Number:c=n===1/0?"; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT":"; max-age="+n;break;case String:c="; expires="+n;break;case Date:c="; expires="+n.toUTCString()}return"rootDomain"!==r&&".rootDomain"!==r||(r=(".rootDomain"===r?".":"")+document.location.hostname.split(".").slice(-2).join(".")),document.cookie=encodeURIComponent(e)+"="+encodeURIComponent(o)+c+(r?"; domain="+r:"")+(t?"; path="+t:"")+(i?"; secure":""),!0}};

					// Implement IAB USP API.
					window.__uspapi = function( command, version, callback ) {

						// Validate callback.
						if ( typeof callback !== 'function' ) {
							return;
						}

						// Validate the given command.
						if ( command !== 'getUSPData' || version !== 1 ) {
							callback( null, false );
							return;
						}

						// Check for GPC. If set, override any stored cookie.
						if ( navigator.globalPrivacyControl ) {
							callback( { version: 1, uspString: '1YYN' }, true );
							return;
						}

						// Check for cookie.
						var consent = cookieLib.getItem( 'usprivacy' );

						// Invalid cookie.
						if ( null === consent ) {
							callback( null, false );
							return;
						}

						// Everything checks out. Fire the provided callback with the consent data.
						callback( { version: 1, uspString: consent }, true );
					};

					// Initialization.
					document.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', function() {

						// Internal functions.
						var setDefaultOptInCookie = function() {
							var value = '1YNN';
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'usprivacy', value, 365 * 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						};

						var setDefaultOptOutCookie = function() {
							var value = '1YYN';
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'usprivacy', value, 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						};

						var setDefaultNotApplicableCookie = function() {
							var value = '1---';
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'usprivacy', value, 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						};

						var setCcpaAppliesCookie = function( applies ) {
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'ccpa_applies', applies, 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						}

						var maybeCallDoNotSellCallback = function() {
							if ( 'function' === typeof window.doNotSellCallback ) {
								return window.doNotSellCallback();
							}

							return false;
						}

						// Look for usprivacy cookie first.
						var usprivacyCookie = cookieLib.getItem( 'usprivacy' );

						// Found a usprivacy cookie.
						if ( null !== usprivacyCookie ) {

							// If the cookie indicates that CCPA does not apply, then bail.
							if ( '1---' === usprivacyCookie ) {
								return;
							}

							// CCPA applies, so call our callback to add Do Not Sell link to the page.
							maybeCallDoNotSellCallback();

							// We're all done, no more processing needed.
							return;
						}

						// We don't have a usprivacy cookie, so check to see if we have a CCPA applies cookie.
						var ccpaCookie = cookieLib.getItem( 'ccpa_applies' );

						// No CCPA applies cookie found, so we'll need to geolocate if this visitor is from California.
						// This needs to happen client side because we do not have region geo data in our $SERVER headers,
						// only country data -- therefore we can't vary cache on the region.
						if ( null === ccpaCookie ) {

							var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
							request.open( 'GET', 'https://public-api.wordpress.com/geo/', true );

							request.onreadystatechange = function () {
								if ( 4 === this.readyState ) {
									if ( 200 === this.status ) {

										// Got a geo response. Parse out the region data.
										var data = JSON.parse( this.response );
										var region      = data.region ? data.region.toLowerCase() : '';
										var ccpa_applies = ['california', 'colorado', 'connecticut', 'delaware', 'indiana', 'iowa', 'montana', 'new jersey', 'oregon', 'tennessee', 'texas', 'utah', 'virginia'].indexOf( region ) > -1;
										// Set CCPA applies cookie. This keeps us from having to make a geo request too frequently.
										setCcpaAppliesCookie( ccpa_applies );

										// Check if CCPA applies to set the proper usprivacy cookie.
										if ( ccpa_applies ) {
											if ( maybeCallDoNotSellCallback() ) {
												// Do Not Sell link added, so set default opt-in.
												setDefaultOptInCookie();
											} else {
												// Failed showing Do Not Sell link as required, so default to opt-OUT just to be safe.
												setDefaultOptOutCookie();
											}
										} else {
											// CCPA does not apply.
											setDefaultNotApplicableCookie();
										}
									} else {
										// Could not geo, so let's assume for now that CCPA applies to be safe.
										setCcpaAppliesCookie( true );
										if ( maybeCallDoNotSellCallback() ) {
											// Do Not Sell link added, so set default opt-in.
											setDefaultOptInCookie();
										} else {
											// Failed showing Do Not Sell link as required, so default to opt-OUT just to be safe.
											setDefaultOptOutCookie();
										}
									}
								}
							};

							// Send the geo request.
							request.send();
						} else {
							// We found a CCPA applies cookie.
							if ( ccpaCookie === 'true' ) {
								if ( maybeCallDoNotSellCallback() ) {
									// Do Not Sell link added, so set default opt-in.
									setDefaultOptInCookie();
								} else {
									// Failed showing Do Not Sell link as required, so default to opt-OUT just to be safe.
									setDefaultOptOutCookie();
								}
							} else {
								// CCPA does not apply.
								setDefaultNotApplicableCookie();
							}
						}
					} );
				};

				// Kickoff initialization.
				if ( window.defQueue && defQueue.isLOHP && defQueue.isLOHP === 2020 ) {
					defQueue.items.push( setupPrivacy );
				} else {
					setupPrivacy();
				}

			} )();
		</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">
		(function () {
			var wpcom_reblog = {
				source: 'toolbar',

				toggle_reblog_box_flair: function (obj_id, post_id) {

					// Go to site selector. This will redirect to their blog if they only have one.
					const postEndpoint = `https://wordpress.com/post`;

					// Ideally we would use the permalink here, but fortunately this will be replaced with the 
					// post permalink in the editor.
					const originalURL = `${ document.location.href }?page_id=${ post_id }`; 
					
					const url =
						postEndpoint +
						'?url=' +
						encodeURIComponent( originalURL ) +
						'&is_post_share=true' +
						'&v=5';

					const redirect = function () {
						if (
							! window.open( url, '_blank' )
						) {
							location.href = url;
						}
					};

					if ( /Firefox/.test( navigator.userAgent ) ) {
						setTimeout( redirect, 0 );
					} else {
						redirect();
					}
				},
			};

			window.wpcom_reblog = wpcom_reblog;
		})();
	</script>

		function addLoadEvent(func) {
			var oldonload = window.onload;
			if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
				window.onload = func;
			} else {
				window.onload = function () {
					oldonload();
					func();
				}
			}
		}

<article id="post-108" class="post-108 page type-page status-publish hentry without-featured-image">
	<header class="entry-header">
		<h1 class="entry-title">Context &#8211; Fantasy</h1>	</header>
		<div class="entry-content">
			<p>Fantasy Mindmap:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="184" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/fantasy-mindmap/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png" data-orig-size="1204,675" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Fantasy Mindmap" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=825" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-184" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=825" alt="Fantasy Mindmap.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png 1204w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=150&amp;h=84 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=300&amp;h=168 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=768&amp;h=431 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=1024&amp;h=574 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1204px) 100vw, 1204px" /></p>
<p>Here are a bunch of words I associate with the word fantasy. I started with words like magic, medieval, heroes as these are words that immediately sprung to mind, following this I went with monsters, dungeons, and towns as these are some other quite common things found in fantasy. With a couple words down on the page I moved onto looking at words I could associate with these, like different types of monsters, things to do with magic, things you&#8217;d find in and around a town like a castle, with castle came kings, queens and knights. A lot of this I find to be very much related to fantasy but most of all would be magic, it is by far one of my favourite things to do with fantasy. Magic is a very vast subject with many different types and forms. Magic has sprung a whole load of different films, books, games, pictures, music, it&#8217;s very closely linked to all media as you have a wide option as to what you want to do.</p>
<p>Tomes Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="189" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/tomes-moodboard-4/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg" data-orig-size="1219,584" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Tomes Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=825" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-189" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=825" alt="Tomes Moodboard.jpg"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg 1219w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=150&amp;h=72 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=300&amp;h=144 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=768&amp;h=368 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=1024&amp;h=491 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1219px) 100vw, 1219px" /></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>The reason I like these images of tomes as a collective is that they all show different styles of designs on the covers as they could have just been a large book. This is the kind of thing I would like to include in my fantasy environment, which would probably be the common shade of green shown above as itâ€™s the most traditional along with the gold to create various detail and designs on the front.</p>
<p>Bows Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="190" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/bows-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1215,584" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Bows Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=825" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-190" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Bows Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png 1215w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=72 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=144 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=369 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=492 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1215px) 100vw, 1215px" /></p>
<p>These Â bows appealed to me as I like the level of appendages on each bow to give it a more grand and special look to it as opposed to a more standard bow which doesnâ€™t look all that interesting. As a collective I like the colours that are used for example the oranges, blues, golds, and yellows. A lot of the images here display bird like features which is another thing that really appealed to me and if I were to include a bow in my environment I would do this myself.</p>
<p>Gargoyles Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="191" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/gargoyles-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1219,568" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Gargoyles Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=825" loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-191" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Gargoyles Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png 1219w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=70 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=140 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=358 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=477 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1219px) 100vw, 1219px" /></p>
<p>Gargoyles have always been a fascinating aspect of gothic architecture due to its many different and unique forms. I like the visuals of these gargoyles as they all display a level of demonic aura which makes for a ominous grin of deceit. This is something that if I were to include a gargoyle into my work would be an aspect of which Iâ€™d aspire to achieve.</p>
<p>Rings Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="192" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/rings-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1222,612" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Rings Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=825" loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-192" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Rings Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png 1222w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=75 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=150 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=385 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=513 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1222px) 100vw, 1222px" /></p>
<p>Here are a selection of images showing rings. I like these rings because they have a very mystical look to them, with the intricate designs and the effective use of jewels they look like magical rings which have been a feature in games featuring magic for a long time, that being if they give a buff or if they cast a spell either one is used frequently. I quite like the idea of having a ring in my diorama if it were to be a magical study or a wizards cabin, or even just in a cave, on the ground as treasure to be found.</p>
<p>Crystals Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="193" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/crystals-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1207,683" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Crystals Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=825" loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-193" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Crystals Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png 1207w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=85 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=170 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=435 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=579 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1207px) 100vw, 1207px" /></p>
<p>I like the idea of having crystals in a fantasy environment, especially if it were to be a crystal cave like scene showing different bright magically crystals in a undisturbed place, a secret abode for fairies and pixies maybe. If I were to have crystals I&#8217;d make them a variety of different colours not just purple and blue, the reason I chose these images is that I like the shapes of them and could use them in my idea, I also like the density of each one maybe with smaller crystals being in larger swarms and larger crystals being on their own.</p>
<p>Caves Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="195" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/caves-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1215,666" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Caves Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=825" loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-195" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Caves Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png 1215w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=82 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=164 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=421 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=561 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1215px) 100vw, 1215px" />Here are some images of caves, the reason I chose these images is that I like the way they depicted a cave. I am quite inspired to create a diorama of a magic cave, as previously shown I would like it to be a crystal cave as it sounds really interesting to me. I would model it after the last two images which show the crystals lighting up the cave and creating a nice ambient light. The variety of shapes will be greatly increased when I do it as I&#8217;d like to have different types of crystal clusters. Despite saying I&#8217;d use different colours I do quite like the purple blue colour scheme as it contrasts nicely.</p>

		<!-- CCPA [start] -->
		<script type="text/javascript">
			( function () {

				var setupPrivacy = function() {

					// Minimal Mozilla Cookie library
					// https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Document/cookie/Simple_document.cookie_framework
					var cookieLib = window.cookieLib = {getItem:function(e){return e&&decodeURIComponent(document.cookie.replace(new RegExp("(?:(?:^|.*;)\\s*"+encodeURIComponent(e).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g,"\\$&")+"\\s*\\=\\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$"),"$1"))||null},setItem:function(e,o,n,t,r,i){if(!e||/^(?:expires|max\-age|path|domain|secure)$/i.test(e))return!1;var c="";if(n)switch(n.constructor){case Number:c=n===1/0?"; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT":"; max-age="+n;break;case String:c="; expires="+n;break;case Date:c="; expires="+n.toUTCString()}return"rootDomain"!==r&&".rootDomain"!==r||(r=(".rootDomain"===r?".":"")+document.location.hostname.split(".").slice(-2).join(".")),document.cookie=encodeURIComponent(e)+"="+encodeURIComponent(o)+c+(r?"; domain="+r:"")+(t?"; path="+t:"")+(i?"; secure":""),!0}};

					// Implement IAB USP API.
					window.__uspapi = function( command, version, callback ) {

						// Validate callback.
						if ( typeof callback !== 'function' ) {
							return;
						}

						// Validate the given command.
						if ( command !== 'getUSPData' || version !== 1 ) {
							callback( null, false );
							return;
						}

						// Check for GPC. If set, override any stored cookie.
						if ( navigator.globalPrivacyControl ) {
							callback( { version: 1, uspString: '1YYN' }, true );
							return;
						}

						// Check for cookie.
						var consent = cookieLib.getItem( 'usprivacy' );

						// Invalid cookie.
						if ( null === consent ) {
							callback( null, false );
							return;
						}

						// Everything checks out. Fire the provided callback with the consent data.
						callback( { version: 1, uspString: consent }, true );
					};

					// Initialization.
					document.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', function() {

						// Internal functions.
						var setDefaultOptInCookie = function() {
							var value = '1YNN';
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'usprivacy', value, 365 * 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						};

						var setDefaultOptOutCookie = function() {
							var value = '1YYN';
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'usprivacy', value, 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						};

						var setDefaultNotApplicableCookie = function() {
							var value = '1---';
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'usprivacy', value, 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						};

						var setCcpaAppliesCookie = function( applies ) {
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'ccpa_applies', applies, 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						}

						var maybeCallDoNotSellCallback = function() {
							if ( 'function' === typeof window.doNotSellCallback ) {
								return window.doNotSellCallback();
							}

							return false;
						}

						// Look for usprivacy cookie first.
						var usprivacyCookie = cookieLib.getItem( 'usprivacy' );

						// Found a usprivacy cookie.
						if ( null !== usprivacyCookie ) {

							// If the cookie indicates that CCPA does not apply, then bail.
							if ( '1---' === usprivacyCookie ) {
								return;
							}

							// CCPA applies, so call our callback to add Do Not Sell link to the page.
							maybeCallDoNotSellCallback();

							// We're all done, no more processing needed.
							return;
						}

						// We don't have a usprivacy cookie, so check to see if we have a CCPA applies cookie.
						var ccpaCookie = cookieLib.getItem( 'ccpa_applies' );

						// No CCPA applies cookie found, so we'll need to geolocate if this visitor is from California.
						// This needs to happen client side because we do not have region geo data in our $SERVER headers,
						// only country data -- therefore we can't vary cache on the region.
						if ( null === ccpaCookie ) {

							var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
							request.open( 'GET', 'https://public-api.wordpress.com/geo/', true );

							request.onreadystatechange = function () {
								if ( 4 === this.readyState ) {
									if ( 200 === this.status ) {

										// Got a geo response. Parse out the region data.
										var data = JSON.parse( this.response );
										var region      = data.region ? data.region.toLowerCase() : '';
										var ccpa_applies = ['california', 'colorado', 'connecticut', 'delaware', 'indiana', 'iowa', 'montana', 'new jersey', 'oregon', 'tennessee', 'texas', 'utah', 'virginia'].indexOf( region ) > -1;
										// Set CCPA applies cookie. This keeps us from having to make a geo request too frequently.
										setCcpaAppliesCookie( ccpa_applies );

										// Check if CCPA applies to set the proper usprivacy cookie.
										if ( ccpa_applies ) {
											if ( maybeCallDoNotSellCallback() ) {
												// Do Not Sell link added, so set default opt-in.
												setDefaultOptInCookie();
											} else {
												// Failed showing Do Not Sell link as required, so default to opt-OUT just to be safe.
												setDefaultOptOutCookie();
											}
										} else {
											// CCPA does not apply.
											setDefaultNotApplicableCookie();
										}
									} else {
										// Could not geo, so let's assume for now that CCPA applies to be safe.
										setCcpaAppliesCookie( true );
										if ( maybeCallDoNotSellCallback() ) {
											// Do Not Sell link added, so set default opt-in.
											setDefaultOptInCookie();
										} else {
											// Failed showing Do Not Sell link as required, so default to opt-OUT just to be safe.
											setDefaultOptOutCookie();
										}
									}
								}
							};

							// Send the geo request.
							request.send();
						} else {
							// We found a CCPA applies cookie.
							if ( ccpaCookie === 'true' ) {
								if ( maybeCallDoNotSellCallback() ) {
									// Do Not Sell link added, so set default opt-in.
									setDefaultOptInCookie();
								} else {
									// Failed showing Do Not Sell link as required, so default to opt-OUT just to be safe.
									setDefaultOptOutCookie();
								}
							} else {
								// CCPA does not apply.
								setDefaultNotApplicableCookie();
							}
						}
					} );
				};

				// Kickoff initialization.
				if ( window.defQueue && defQueue.isLOHP && defQueue.isLOHP === 2020 ) {
					defQueue.items.push( setupPrivacy );
				} else {
					setupPrivacy();
				}

			} )();
		</script>

		<!-- CCPA [end] -->

		(function () {
			var wpcom_reblog = {
				source: 'toolbar',

				toggle_reblog_box_flair: function (obj_id, post_id) {

					// Go to site selector. This will redirect to their blog if they only have one.
					const postEndpoint = `https://wordpress.com/post`;

					// Ideally we would use the permalink here, but fortunately this will be replaced with the 
					// post permalink in the editor.
					const originalURL = `${ document.location.href }?page_id=${ post_id }`; 
					
					const url =
						postEndpoint +
						'?url=' +
						encodeURIComponent( originalURL ) +
						'&is_post_share=true' +
						'&v=5';

					const redirect = function () {
						if (
							! window.open( url, '_blank' )
						) {
							location.href = url;
						}
					};

					if ( /Firefox/.test( navigator.userAgent ) ) {
						setTimeout( redirect, 0 );
					} else {
						redirect();
					}
				},
			};

			window.wpcom_reblog = wpcom_reblog;
		})();
	</script>

		function addLoadEvent(func) {
			var oldonload = window.onload;
			if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
				window.onload = func;
			} else {
				window.onload = function () {
					oldonload();
					func();
				}
			}
		}

					'a[href="https://wordpress.com/?ref=footer_website"]',
					'a[href="https://wordpress.com/?ref=vertical_footer"]',

					return false;

<article id="post-108" class="post-108 page type-page status-publish hentry without-featured-image">
	<header class="entry-header">
		<h1 class="entry-title">Context &#8211; Fantasy</h1>	</header>
		<div class="entry-content">
			<p>Fantasy Mindmap:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="184" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/fantasy-mindmap/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png" data-orig-size="1204,675" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Fantasy Mindmap" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=825" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-184" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=825" alt="Fantasy Mindmap.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png 1204w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=150&amp;h=84 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=300&amp;h=168 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=768&amp;h=431 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/fantasy-mindmap.png?w=1024&amp;h=574 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1204px) 100vw, 1204px" /></p>
<p>Here are a bunch of words I associate with the word fantasy. I started with words like magic, medieval, heroes as these are words that immediately sprung to mind, following this I went with monsters, dungeons, and towns as these are some other quite common things found in fantasy. With a couple words down on the page I moved onto looking at words I could associate with these, like different types of monsters, things to do with magic, things you&#8217;d find in and around a town like a castle, with castle came kings, queens and knights. A lot of this I find to be very much related to fantasy but most of all would be magic, it is by far one of my favourite things to do with fantasy. Magic is a very vast subject with many different types and forms. Magic has sprung a whole load of different films, books, games, pictures, music, it&#8217;s very closely linked to all media as you have a wide option as to what you want to do.</p>
<p>Tomes Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="189" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/tomes-moodboard-4/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg" data-orig-size="1219,584" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Tomes Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=825" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-189" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=825" alt="Tomes Moodboard.jpg"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg 1219w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=150&amp;h=72 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=300&amp;h=144 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=768&amp;h=368 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/tomes-moodboard.jpg?w=1024&amp;h=491 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1219px) 100vw, 1219px" /></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>The reason I like these images of tomes as a collective is that they all show different styles of designs on the covers as they could have just been a large book. This is the kind of thing I would like to include in my fantasy environment, which would probably be the common shade of green shown above as itâ€™s the most traditional along with the gold to create various detail and designs on the front.</p>
<p>Bows Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="190" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/bows-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1215,584" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Bows Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=825" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-190" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Bows Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png 1215w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=72 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=144 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=369 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/bows-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=492 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1215px) 100vw, 1215px" /></p>
<p>These Â bows appealed to me as I like the level of appendages on each bow to give it a more grand and special look to it as opposed to a more standard bow which doesnâ€™t look all that interesting. As a collective I like the colours that are used for example the oranges, blues, golds, and yellows. A lot of the images here display bird like features which is another thing that really appealed to me and if I were to include a bow in my environment I would do this myself.</p>
<p>Gargoyles Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="191" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/gargoyles-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1219,568" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Gargoyles Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=825" loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-191" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Gargoyles Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png 1219w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=70 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=140 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=358 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/gargoyles-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=477 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1219px) 100vw, 1219px" /></p>
<p>Gargoyles have always been a fascinating aspect of gothic architecture due to its many different and unique forms. I like the visuals of these gargoyles as they all display a level of demonic aura which makes for a ominous grin of deceit. This is something that if I were to include a gargoyle into my work would be an aspect of which Iâ€™d aspire to achieve.</p>
<p>Rings Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="192" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/rings-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1222,612" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Rings Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=825" loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-192" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Rings Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png 1222w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=75 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=150 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=385 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/rings-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=513 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1222px) 100vw, 1222px" /></p>
<p>Here are a selection of images showing rings. I like these rings because they have a very mystical look to them, with the intricate designs and the effective use of jewels they look like magical rings which have been a feature in games featuring magic for a long time, that being if they give a buff or if they cast a spell either one is used frequently. I quite like the idea of having a ring in my diorama if it were to be a magical study or a wizards cabin, or even just in a cave, on the ground as treasure to be found.</p>
<p>Crystals Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="193" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/crystals-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1207,683" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Crystals Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=825" loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-193" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Crystals Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png 1207w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=85 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=170 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=435 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/crystals-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=579 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1207px) 100vw, 1207px" /></p>
<p>I like the idea of having crystals in a fantasy environment, especially if it were to be a crystal cave like scene showing different bright magically crystals in a undisturbed place, a secret abode for fairies and pixies maybe. If I were to have crystals I&#8217;d make them a variety of different colours not just purple and blue, the reason I chose these images is that I like the shapes of them and could use them in my idea, I also like the density of each one maybe with smaller crystals being in larger swarms and larger crystals being on their own.</p>
<p>Caves Moodboard:</p>
<p><img data-attachment-id="195" data-permalink="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/context-fantasy/caves-moodboard/" data-orig-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png" data-orig-size="1215,666" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Caves Moodboard" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=300" data-large-file="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=825" loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-195" src="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=825" alt="Caves Moodboard.png"   srcset="https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png 1215w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=150&amp;h=82 150w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=300&amp;h=164 300w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=768&amp;h=421 768w, https://hematemimi2.wordpress.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/caves-moodboard.png?w=1024&amp;h=561 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 1215px) 100vw, 1215px" />Here are some images of caves, the reason I chose these images is that I like the way they depicted a cave. I am quite inspired to create a diorama of a magic cave, as previously shown I would like it to be a crystal cave as it sounds really interesting to me. I would model it after the last two images which show the crystals lighting up the cave and creating a nice ambient light. The variety of shapes will be greatly increased when I do it as I&#8217;d like to have different types of crystal clusters. Despite saying I&#8217;d use different colours I do quite like the purple blue colour scheme as it contrasts nicely.</p>

		<!-- CCPA [start] -->
		<script type="text/javascript">
			( function () {

				var setupPrivacy = function() {

					// Minimal Mozilla Cookie library
					// https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Document/cookie/Simple_document.cookie_framework
					var cookieLib = window.cookieLib = {getItem:function(e){return e&&decodeURIComponent(document.cookie.replace(new RegExp("(?:(?:^|.*;)\\s*"+encodeURIComponent(e).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g,"\\$&")+"\\s*\\=\\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$"),"$1"))||null},setItem:function(e,o,n,t,r,i){if(!e||/^(?:expires|max\-age|path|domain|secure)$/i.test(e))return!1;var c="";if(n)switch(n.constructor){case Number:c=n===1/0?"; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT":"; max-age="+n;break;case String:c="; expires="+n;break;case Date:c="; expires="+n.toUTCString()}return"rootDomain"!==r&&".rootDomain"!==r||(r=(".rootDomain"===r?".":"")+document.location.hostname.split(".").slice(-2).join(".")),document.cookie=encodeURIComponent(e)+"="+encodeURIComponent(o)+c+(r?"; domain="+r:"")+(t?"; path="+t:"")+(i?"; secure":""),!0}};

					// Implement IAB USP API.
					window.__uspapi = function( command, version, callback ) {

						// Validate callback.
						if ( typeof callback !== 'function' ) {
							return;
						}

						// Validate the given command.
						if ( command !== 'getUSPData' || version !== 1 ) {
							callback( null, false );
							return;
						}

						// Check for GPC. If set, override any stored cookie.
						if ( navigator.globalPrivacyControl ) {
							callback( { version: 1, uspString: '1YYN' }, true );
							return;
						}

						// Check for cookie.
						var consent = cookieLib.getItem( 'usprivacy' );

						// Invalid cookie.
						if ( null === consent ) {
							callback( null, false );
							return;
						}

						// Everything checks out. Fire the provided callback with the consent data.
						callback( { version: 1, uspString: consent }, true );
					};

					// Initialization.
					document.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', function() {

						// Internal functions.
						var setDefaultOptInCookie = function() {
							var value = '1YNN';
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'usprivacy', value, 365 * 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						};

						var setDefaultOptOutCookie = function() {
							var value = '1YYN';
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'usprivacy', value, 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						};

						var setDefaultNotApplicableCookie = function() {
							var value = '1---';
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'usprivacy', value, 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						};

						var setCcpaAppliesCookie = function( applies ) {
							var domain = '.wordpress.com' === location.hostname.slice( -14 ) ? '.rootDomain' : location.hostname;
							cookieLib.setItem( 'ccpa_applies', applies, 24 * 60 * 60, '/', domain );
						}

						var maybeCallDoNotSellCallback = function() {
							if ( 'function' === typeof window.doNotSellCallback ) {
								return window.doNotSellCallback();
							}

							return false;
						}

						// Look for usprivacy cookie first.
						var usprivacyCookie = cookieLib.getItem( 'usprivacy' );

						// Found a usprivacy cookie.
						if ( null !== usprivacyCookie ) {

							// If the cookie indicates that CCPA does not apply, then bail.
							if ( '1---' === usprivacyCookie ) {
								return;
							}

							// CCPA applies, so call our callback to add Do Not Sell link to the page.
							maybeCallDoNotSellCallback();

							// We're all done, no more processing needed.
							return;
						}

						// We don't have a usprivacy cookie, so check to see if we have a CCPA applies cookie.
						var ccpaCookie = cookieLib.getItem( 'ccpa_applies' );

						// No CCPA applies cookie found, so we'll need to geolocate if this visitor is from California.
						// This needs to happen client side because we do not have region geo data in our $SERVER headers,
						// only country data -- therefore we can't vary cache on the region.
						if ( null === ccpaCookie ) {

							var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
							request.open( 'GET', 'https://public-api.wordpress.com/geo/', true );

							request.onreadystatechange = function () {
								if ( 4 === this.readyState ) {
									if ( 200 === this.status ) {

										// Got a geo response. Parse out the region data.
										var data = JSON.parse( this.response );
										var region      = data.region ? data.region.toLowerCase() : '';
										var ccpa_applies = ['california', 'colorado', 'connecticut', 'delaware', 'indiana', 'iowa', 'montana', 'new jersey', 'oregon', 'tennessee', 'texas', 'utah', 'virginia'].indexOf( region ) > -1;
										// Set CCPA applies cookie. This keeps us from having to make a geo request too frequently.
										setCcpaAppliesCookie( ccpa_applies );

										// Check if CCPA applies to set the proper usprivacy cookie.
										if ( ccpa_applies ) {
											if ( maybeCallDoNotSellCallback() ) {
												// Do Not Sell link added, so set default opt-in.
												setDefaultOptInCookie();
											} else {
												// Failed showing Do Not Sell link as required, so default to opt-OUT just to be safe.
												setDefaultOptOutCookie();
											}
										} else {
											// CCPA does not apply.
											setDefaultNotApplicableCookie();
										}
									} else {
										// Could not geo, so let's assume for now that CCPA applies to be safe.
										setCcpaAppliesCookie( true );
										if ( maybeCallDoNotSellCallback() ) {
											// Do Not Sell link added, so set default opt-in.
											setDefaultOptInCookie();
										} else {
											// Failed showing Do Not Sell link as required, so default to opt-OUT just to be safe.
											setDefaultOptOutCookie();
										}
									}
								}
							};

							// Send the geo request.
							request.send();
						} else {
							// We found a CCPA applies cookie.
							if ( ccpaCookie === 'true' ) {
								if ( maybeCallDoNotSellCallback() ) {
									// Do Not Sell link added, so set default opt-in.
									setDefaultOptInCookie();
								} else {
									// Failed showing Do Not Sell link as required, so default to opt-OUT just to be safe.
									setDefaultOptOutCookie();
								}
							} else {
								// CCPA does not apply.
								setDefaultNotApplicableCookie();
							}
						}
					} );
				};

				// Kickoff initialization.
				if ( window.defQueue && defQueue.isLOHP && defQueue.isLOHP === 2020 ) {
					defQueue.items.push( setupPrivacy );
				} else {
					setupPrivacy();
				}

			} )();
		</script>

		<!-- CCPA [end] -->

	<script type="text/javascript">
		(function () {
			var wpcom_reblog = {
				source: 'toolbar',

				toggle_reblog_box_flair: function (obj_id, post_id) {

					// Go to site selector. This will redirect to their blog if they only have one.
					const postEndpoint = `https://wordpress.com/post`;

					// Ideally we would use the permalink here, but fortunately this will be replaced with the 
					// post permalink in the editor.
					const originalURL = `${ document.location.href }?page_id=${ post_id }`; 
					
					const url =
						postEndpoint +
						'?url=' +
						encodeURIComponent( originalURL ) +
						'&is_post_share=true' +
						'&v=5';

					const redirect = function () {
						if (
							! window.open( url, '_blank' )
						) {
							location.href = url;
						}
					};

					if ( /Firefox/.test( navigator.userAgent ) ) {
						setTimeout( redirect, 0 );
					} else {
						redirect();
					}
				},
			};

			window.wpcom_reblog = wpcom_reblog;
		})();
	</script>

		function addLoadEvent(func) {
			var oldonload = window.onload;
			if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
				window.onload = func;
			} else {
				window.onload = function () {
					oldonload();

				}
